Comment: themusicroomatmidway said "Super excited to be playing "The Amazing Note Race" with third grade today!! We have been learning about the note names on the treble staff, and today we are reviewing by playing this awesome game. The kids will be in two teams. While the music plays, they will pass the tater tot. When the music stops, I'll display a note on the board. The person who has the tot must run and put the tot on the correct note name and get back to their spot before their competitor does. Whoever is first with the correct answer gets the point, and the first team to 20 points wins tickets! #themusicroomatmidway #musiceducation #musiced #musiceducationmatters #fun #elementarymusic"

Comment: themusicroomatmidway said "Super excited to be playing "The Amazing Note Race" with third grade today!! We have been learning about the note names on the treble staff, and today we are reviewing by playing this awesome game. The kids will be in two teams. While the music plays, they will pass the tater tot. When the music stops, I'll display a note on the board. The person who has the tot must run and put the tot on the correct note name and get back to their spot before their competitor does. Whoever is first with the correct answer gets the point, and the first team to 20 points wins tickets! #themusicroomatmidway #musiceducation #musiced #musiceducationmatters #fun #elementarymusic"

*Available ONLY to 501c(3) Rescue Organizations by rules of Caddo Parish Animal Services and Mosquito Control, located at 1500 Monty Street Shreveport, LOUISIANA 71107. THIS Companions of Caddo Animal Servicesï»¿ PAGE IS RUN BY VOLUNTEERS, not employees of the shelter.

3/3/15 UPDATE: 
On 2/27/15 Friday, Humane Society of Northwest Louisiana pulled 1

On 3/2/15 Monday,
-Ninna's Road to Rescue - Benton, Louisiana pulled 2
-Pet Savers of Shreveport pulled 6
-Louisiana Dog Rescue pulled 2
-Angel's Heart Puppy Rescue pulled 8
-Stop Animal Cruelty in Hot Spring County (Arkansas) pulled 6

On 3/3/15 Tuesday,
- Humane Society of Northwest Louisiana pulled an additional 2 (the mother & baby that originally were not allowed to be pulled by rescues)

If you are interested in fostering or adopting any of the dogs pictured, please contact one of the rescues listed above.
We are hearing there are ONLY 4 LEFT in need of 501c3 rescue organizations. 
The shelter has told us 10-12 dogs from this same group seized will go up for adoption later in the week. For adoptions, you have to go in person to the shelter. $50 cash fee. You can also call the Caddo Parish Animal Shelter at 318-226-6624. There's a chance some of the 10-12 selected for adoption may end up in "Rescue Only" too as they are pending vet examinations."" via @PhotoRepost_app @jojoandgilbert @dixie812 @they_matter"

3/3/15 UPDATE: 
On 2/27/15 Friday, Humane Society of Northwest Louisiana pulled 1

On 3/2/15 Monday,
-Ninna's Road to Rescue - Benton, Louisiana pulled 2
-Pet Savers of Shreveport pulled 6
-Louisiana Dog Rescue pulled 2
-Angel's Heart Puppy Rescue pulled 8
-Stop Animal Cruelty in Hot Spring County (Arkansas) pulled 6

On 3/3/15 Tuesday,
- Humane Society of Northwest Louisiana pulled an additional 2 (the mother & baby that originally were not allowed to be pulled by rescues)

If you are interested in fostering or adopting any of the dogs pictured, please contact one of the rescues listed above.
We are hearing there are ONLY 4 LEFT in need of 501c3 rescue organizations. 
The shelter has told us 10-12 dogs from this same group seized will go up for adoption later in the week. For adoptions, you have to go in person to the shelter. $50 cash fee. You can also call the Caddo Parish Animal Shelter at 318-226-6624. There's a chance some of the 10-12 selected for adoption may end up in "Rescue Only" too as they are pending vet examinations."" via @PhotoRepost_app @jojoandgilbert @dixie812 @they_matter"
